posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:The overall feeling of the accommodation is as follows:
1. In terms of environmental decoration, the hotel opened in 2019 and is very new. The layout of the guest room and the washing area is very good, and there is an iron. There is a porch at the entrance where you can sit down and change shoes comfortably. The living room and bedroom are all covered with soft carpets. Dry and wet separation. The decoration is very suitable for modern, clean, comfortable and young people. I like the decoration of the Crown store very much. The actual environment is more comfortable and refreshing than the feeling in the picture. In terms of hot water, the temperature of the hot water for bathing is very hot, which can wash away the fatigue of a day. If you have requirements for the temperature of hot water, this hotel will definitely meet it. This is something that those small shops, homestays, etc. cannot meet. The difference between five-star hotels and other non-star hotels lies in the subtle differences in hot water supply systems, decoration materials, bedding, hygiene, safety, hotel room layout, etc.
2. Food. When placing an order on Ctrip, a dinner buffet at the hotel's western restaurant was included. After visiting Dongzha and Xizha in a punch-in style, I rushed back to the hotel at 8 o'clock (end at 9 o'clock). The style is very rich. I have to say that the salmon in this hotel is delicious. üòã, recommended~~ There is also protein-rich beef for dinner, as well as pepper pork belly and chicken soup, which is very warm and will definitely satisfy meat lovers; the point is that the breakfast is very rich, and I have to say that the coffee here is really delicious: the latte is really delicious, there are 3 coffee machines, although the coffee machine is inconspicuous, but the beans used in this place are very mellow and delicious, not inferior to the big coffee shops. Better than Starbucks. As a person who likes and has drunk Austrian Vienna coffee, the coffee of Crowne Plaza Wuzhen can satisfy the coffee stomach of Chinese people. Latte is not bitter or astringent, and has a milky taste. A cup in the morning will refresh your mind and your taste buds will be absolutely satisfiedüòå. According to the lady serving in the hotel restaurant, their beans are carefully selected. I have been on so many business trips and stayed in so many hotels. Crowne Plaza Wuzhen has made a sincere effort in coffee and food, and I really like it. On the third day of the May Day holiday, during the peak period, the guest rooms were almost full, and the breakfast room was full (open until 10:30), but the hotel still arranged breakfast for the guests in an orderly manner. The key is that if the guests want to pack the coffee in the breakfast room to the room, they are allowed to do so. I am really touched. It is worthy of the five-star service. Some five-star hotels do not allow packaging. I really like it üëçüëçüëç. It can be seen that the coffee is so delicious that people want to pack it. However, the coffee is delicious, so it is not recommended to be greedy. I also hope that the store will retain this service, maintain the good taste of coffee, and make it a special sign of Crowne Plaza Wuzhen. I took a few photos of coffee to commemorate this and put them up to prove that the hotel's service is indeed like this; the third thing that left a good impression was the bread in the morning, which was the kind that was cut. It seemed to be called baguette, but it was not as hard as baguette. The crust was very crispy, but the bread was very soft. After spreading butter, the taste of wheat met the mellow aroma of milk fat. It was really delicious. After eating three small pieces, I couldn't help but cut three small pieces again. With coffee, I was really healed by food. In addition, the pork belly and lean meat in the tofu knot roast meat are also very tasty üòãüòã. The salmon, coffee and breakfast bread at Crowne Plaza Wuzhen are really good for Western food lovers üëç. I recommend friends who like the above food to try it.
3. Transportation: The hotel itself is about 10 minutes' walk from the Dongzha Scenic Area (no need to take a taxi, you can walk there); there is a K350 bus from the Dongzha Scenic Area to the Xizha (main scenic spot), which is very convenient. Just open the Jiaxing QR code for taking the bus, use Alipay, and the bus does not support the WeChat traffic QR code. During the peak holiday season, the taxi price is 50 yuan (from Xizha to the hotel), but it is only about 3 kilometers away. Be patient and wait for the Tongxiang Night Tour No. 010 bus. Basically, you can get back to the hotel from Xizha in half an hour (the stop is "Wuzhen Bus Station"). Wuzhen Bus Station is just a road intersection on the left hand side of the hotel, 3-5 minutes away, very close and very convenient. In addition, Wuzhen Bus Station has a fixed intercity bus that goes directly to Hangzhou Xiaoshan Airport, with an average of one trip per hour, which is very convenient. It takes about 2 hours to reach Hangzhou Xiaoshan Airport by car, which is very convenient and the bus is also very clean. The "Baba Express" WeChat public account and mini program can both purchase buses from Wuzhen Bus Station to Hangzhou Xiaoshan Airport, which is much more convenient than the high-speed rail.
4. Hotel fitness facilities: There are swimming pools, treadmills and other equipment, and the key point is that the gym is 24 hours.
5. If you don‚Äôt want to live in the Xizha Scenic Area during the peak holidays or be raised by small homestays, you can book the Crowne Plaza Wuzhen on the premise of sufficient budget. The price-performance ratio and comfort are really good, üòÄüòÄ.
6. Suggested improvements: The pillows are relatively soft, and you can consider equipping some buckwheat pillows or latex pillows. More towels and drinking water can be placed in the gym. Although everyone comes to take a vacation to visit attractions, there will not be too many fitness guests in the store.
It was a really satisfying journey, and the hotel I chose was very good. It was a really satisfying accommodation experience and vacation. I will choose this hotel next time I go to Wuzhen.
